Never again touch the mouse and keyboard, or touchscreen, when using this best speech to text app.\r\n\r\nSpeech to text technology is not perfect and mistakes do happen. You may tell a speech-to-text app \"pun not intended\" and it might print \"pun not in ten did\".\r\n\r\nSpeechToText Pro offers about 45 voice commands referred to as Actions. You can use them to select, edit, insert, delete or modify any segment of text. You can also assign your own voice commands to an Action. \r\n\r\nSome of those Actions are: Select [word], Select from [word1] until [word2], Insert [word] before/after [some word], Delete [word], Capitalize [word], Round bracket [word], Select last sentence, and more. Voice commands replace the mouse and keyboard. However, the option to modify text using those methods exists too.\r\n\r\n3) Let you substitute the predefined voice commands with your own.\r\n\r\n4) Offer support for hotkeys. Simply assign a voice command to a difficult-to-pronounce segment of text. Then pronounce the voice command for the difficult-to-pronounce text to print.\r\n\r\n5) Let you save text, send it as an email, send it as an SMS message, share it to other apps, upload it to OneDrive, play it back in a synthetic voice, or print it.\r\n\r\n6) Provide a convenient user interface for paraphrasing spoken content in Youtube videos.\r\n\r\n7) Let you do scientific calculator-level calculations with its voice-driven calculator.\r\n\r\n8) Help you protect your content by defining users. \r\n\r\n9) Allow you to produce richly formatted content that can be saved as an RTF file, PDF file, or printed. \r\n\r\nAlthough SpeechToText Pro has a learning curve, it is minimized thanks to its intuitive design, easy-to-read documentation, and the fact that every control (button, switch, menu) throughout the user interface is documented with a tooltip.
